===== 1) FRONTEND: hipiplayServerApi.ts =====
const envServerUrl = (
  import.meta as unknown as {
    env?: {
      VITE_HIPIPLAY_SERVER_URL?: string;
    };
  }
).env?.VITE_HIPIPLAY_SERVER_URL;

export const HIPIPLAY_SERVER_URL = (envServerUrl || '').replace(/\/$/, '');

export type ServerPhase = 'BETTING' | 'RACE' | 'RESULTS';

export type ServerHorse = {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  color: string;
};

export type ServerTotal = {
  horseId: number;
  name: string;
  color: string;
  totalAmount: number;
  totalBets: number;
};

export type ServerWinner = {
  position: number;
  horseId: number;
  name: string;
  color: string;
  totalAmount?: number;
  totalBets?: number;
};

export type ServerRaceState = {
  ok: boolean;
  serverTime: number;
  roundId: number;
  raceNumber?: number;
  phase: ServerPhase;
  secondsRemaining: number;
  bettingSeconds: number;
  raceSeconds: number;
  resultsSeconds?: number;
  payoutMultiplier?: number;
  raceStartedAt: number | null;
  resultsStartedAt?: number | null;
  horses: ServerHorse[];
  totals?: ServerTotal[];
  totalBetsReceived: number;
  winners: ServerWinner[];
};

export type ServerBetPayload = {
  playerId: string;
  horseId: number;
  amount: number;
  balanceApostado: number;
  balanceTotal: number;
  clientName?: string;
};

export type ServerBetResponse = {
  ok: boolean;
  message?: string;
  error?: string;
  bet?: {
    id: string;
    roundId?: number;
    raceNumber?: number;
    playerId: string;
    clientName?: string;
    horseId: number;
    horseName?: string;
    amount?: number;
    balanceApostado?: number;
    balanceTotal?: number;
    balanceBeforeBet?: number;
    balanceAfterBet?: number;
    serverBalance?: number;
    createdAt?: string;
  };
  state?: ServerRaceState;
};

export type ServerPublicRaceHistory = {
  raceNumber: number;
  winners: number[];
};

export type ServerHistoryResponse = {
  ok: boolean;
  history: ServerPublicRaceHistory[];
};

export type ServerPlayerBalance = {
  ok: boolean;
  playerId: string;
  balance: number;
  serverManaged: boolean;
};

export type ServerPlayerSettlement = {
  betId: string;
  horseId: number;
  horseName?: string;
  amount: number;
  balanceBeforeBet?: number;
  balanceAfterBet?: number;
  won: boolean;
  payout: number;
  finalBalance?: number;
  multiplier?: number;
};

export type ServerPlayerResult = {
  ok: boolean;
  available: boolean;
  raceNumber?: number;
  roundId?: number;
  playerId: string;
  won?: boolean;
  totalBetAmount?: number;
  totalPayout?: number;
  multiplier?: number;
  phase?: string;
  message?: string;
  balanceBeforeBet?: number | null;
  balanceAfterBet?: number | null;
  finalBalance?: number | null;
  winners?: {
    position: number;
    horseId: number;
    name?: string;
    color?: string;
  }[];
  settlements?: ServerPlayerSettlement[];
};

async function readJsonResponse<T>(response: Response, fallbackMessage: string): Promise<T> {
  let data: any = null;

  try {
    data = await response.json();
  } catch {
    data = null;
  }

  if (!response.ok || data?.ok === false) {
    throw new Error(data?.error || data?.message || `${fallbackMessage}. HTTP ${response.status}`);
  }

  return data as T;
}

export async function getServerRaceState(): Promise<ServerRaceState> {
  const response = await fetch(`${HIPIPLAY_SERVER_URL}/api/state`, {
    method: 'GET',
    cache: 'no-store',
    headers: {
      Accept: 'application/json'
    }
  });

  const data = await readJsonResponse<ServerRaceState>(response, 'No se pudo consultar el servidor');

  if (!data?.ok) {
    throw new Error('El servidor respondió un estado inválido.');
  }

  return data;
}

export async function sendServerBet(payload: ServerBetPayload): Promise<ServerBetResponse> {
  const response = await fetch(`${HIPIPLAY_SERVER_URL}/api/bet`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      Accept: 'application/json',
      'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
  });

  return readJsonResponse<ServerBetResponse>(response, 'No se pudo registrar la apuesta');
}

export async function getServerRaceHistory(): Promise<ServerPublicRaceHistory[]> {
  const response = await fetch(`${HIPIPLAY_SERVER_URL}/api/history`, {
    method: 'GET',
    cache: 'no-store',
    headers: {
      Accept: 'application/json'
    }
  });

  const data = await readJsonResponse<ServerHistoryResponse>(response, 'No se pudo consultar el historial del servidor');

  if (!Array.isArray(data.history)) {
    throw new Error('El servidor respondió un historial inválido.');
  }

  return data.history;
}

export async function getServerPlayerBalance(playerId: string): Promise<ServerPlayerBalance> {
  const response = await fetch(`${HIPIPLAY_SERVER_URL}/api/player/balance/${encodeURIComponent(playerId)}`, {
    method: 'GET',
    cache: 'no-store',
    headers: {
      Accept: 'application/json'
    }
  });

  const data = await readJsonResponse<ServerPlayerBalance>(response, 'No se pudo consultar el balance del jugador');

  if (!Number.isFinite(Number(data.balance))) {
    throw new Error('El servidor respondió un balance inválido.');
  }

  return {
    ...data,
    balance: Math.max(0, Math.floor(Number(data.balance)))
  };
}

export async function getServerPlayerResult(playerId: string): Promise<ServerPlayerResult> {
  const response = await fetch(`${HIPIPLAY_SERVER_URL}/api/player/result/${encodeURIComponent(playerId)}`, {
    method: 'GET',
    cache: 'no-store',
    headers: {
      Accept: 'application/json'
    }
  });

  return readJsonResponse<ServerPlayerResult>(response, 'No se pudo consultar el resultado del jugador');
}

export function getServerTop3(state: ServerRaceState | null): number[] {
  if (!state?.winners?.length) return [];

  return [...state.winners]
    .sort((a, b) => Number(a.position || 0) - Number(b.position || 0))
    .map((winner) => Number(winner.horseId))
    .filter((horseId) => Number.isFinite(horseId))
    .slice(0, 3);
}
